NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

Adhi Dravidar Colony, Edayansathu, Thorapadi, Vellore-632 002, after the biological change, has been reared as a femalereference, Dr. Angeline Selvaraj MBBS, MS Reg. No. 42298, Assistant Professor, Plastic Surgery, Government Kilpauk

be reared as female I G.V. Diwakar shall henceforth be known as G.V. RUTH DEEVA.
